<div markdown class="api-header">

# Grist API Reference

REST API for manipulating documents, workspaces, and team sites.

- [API Usage](rest-api.md) is an introduction to using the API.
- [API Console](https://docs.getgrist.com/apiconsole) allows you to make API calls from the browser.
</div>

        " fill="currentColor"></path></g></svg></div></div><div class="sc-jtiXyc dUnYDK api-content"><div class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw api-info"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs sc-dFRpbK jBVWZw fdKBSs">Grist API<!-- --> <span>(<!-- -->1.0.1<!-- -->)</span></h1><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"></div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt" data-role="redoc-summary"></div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt" data-role="redoc-description"><p>An API for manipulating Grist sites, workspaces, and documents.</p>
</div></div></div></div><div id="section/Authentication" data-section-id="section/Authentication" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs jBVWZw"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#section/Authentication" aria-label="section/Authentication"></a>Authentication</h1></div></div><div id="section/Authentication/ApiKey" data-section-id="section/Authentication/ApiKey" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM ejDbYC"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#section/Authentication/ApiKey" aria-label="section/Authentication/ApiKey"></a>ApiKey</h2><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"><p>Access to the Grist API is controlled by an Authorization header, which should contain the word &#39;Bearer&#39;, followed by a space, followed by your API key.</p>
</div><div class="sc-gsWcmt gFFElt"><div class="sc-GvhzO hbgnvk"><b>Security Scheme Type: </b><span>HTTP</span></div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"><div class="sc-GvhzO hbgnvk"><b>HTTP Authorization Scheme: </b><code>bearer</code></div><div class="sc-GvhzO hbgnvk"><b>Bearer format: </b><code>Authorization: Bearer XXXXXXXXXXX</code></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/orgs" data-section-id="tag/orgs" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs jBVWZw"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/orgs" aria-label="tag/orgs"></a>orgs</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN fydXJm"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt redoc-markdown "><p>Team sites and personal spaces are called &#39;orgs&#39; in the API.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs" data-section-id="tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/listOrgs" id="operation/listOrgs" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM ejDbYC"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs" aria-label="tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs"></a>List the orgs you have access to<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN cjZEpp http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT gWMowg">/orgs</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dFHjgH"><span>https://{gristhost}/api</span>/orgs</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGkqmO hCTIhr"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"><p>This enumerates all the team sites or personal areas available.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf dVTqCh"><span class="sc-dsXzNU A-DJqO"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh lbYftx"><svg class="sc-dIsUp dqYXmg" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC kdwQRp"><p>An array of organizations</p>
</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy jeBHqu gcushC"><div><h3 class="sc-kEqXSa iXmHCl"> <!-- -->Response samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-cxNHIi gxohHo" </div><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT sc-gSYDnn fQMiLF doEmFO bvejIk" kind="field" title="delta"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><button aria-label="expand properties"><span class="property-name">delta</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp hGHhhO" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">object</span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-eJocfa jWaWWE bArHDh"> (<!-- -->DocAccessWrite<!-- -->) </span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"></div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh jUGDyD" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC kdwQRp"><p>Success</p>
</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy jeBHqu gcushC"><div><h3 class="sc-kEqXSa iXmHCl"> <!-- -->Request samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-cxNHIi gxohHo" </span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy jeBHqu gcushC"></div></div></div><div id="tag/docs/operation/downloadTableSchema" data-section-id="tag/docs/operation/downloadTableSchema" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/downloadTableSchema" id="operation/downloadTableSchema" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM ejDbYC"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/docs/operation/downloadTableSchema" aria-label="tag/docs/operation/downloadTableSchema"></a>The schema of a table<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN cjZEpp http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT gWMowg">/docs/{docId}/download/table-schema</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dFHjgH"><span>https://{gristhost}/api</span>/docs/{docId}/download/table-schema</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGkqmO hCTIhr"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"><p>The schema follows <a href="https://specs.frictionlessdata.io/table-schema/">frictionlessdata&#39;s table-schema standard</a>.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf dVTqCh"><span class="sc-dsXzNU A-DJqO"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>

12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf dVTqCh"><span class="sc-dsXzNU A-DJqO"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>normalized table name (see <code>TABLE ID</code> in Raw Data) or numeric row ID in <code>_grist_Tables</code></p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="hidden"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">hidden</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Set to true to include the hidden columns (like &quot;manualSort&quot;)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="X-Limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">X-Limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Same as <code>limit</code> query parameter.</p>

</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="onmany"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">onmany</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Enum<!-- -->:</span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">&quot;first&quot;</span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">&quot;none&quot;</span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">&quot;all&quot;</span> </div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Which records to update if multiple records are found to match <code>require</code>.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>first</code> - the first matching record (default)</li>
<li><code>none</code> - do not update anything</li>
<li><code>all</code> - update all matches</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="noadd"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">noadd</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Set to true to prohibit adding records.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="noupdate"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">noupdate</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Set to true to prohibit updating records.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="allow_empty_require"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">allow_empty_require</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Set to true to allow <code>require</code> in the body to be empty, which will match and update all records in the table.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-cBoqAE eKyrDP">application/json</span></h5><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"><p>The records to add or update. Instead of an id, a <code>require</code> object is provided, with the same structure as <code>fields</code>. If no query parameter options are set, then the operation is as follows. First, we check if a record exists matching the values specified for columns in <code>require</code>. If so, we update it by setting the values specified for columns in <code>fields</code>. If not, we create a new record with a combination of the values in <code>require</code> and <code>fields</code>, with <code>fields</code> taking priority if the same column is specified in both. The query parameters allow for variations on this behavior.</p>
</div><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT sc-gSYDnn fQMiLF doEmFO bvejIk" kind="field" title="records"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><button aria-label="expand properties"><span class="property-name">records</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp hGHhhO" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa">Array of </span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">objects</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"></div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh jUGDyD" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC kdwQRp"><p>Success</p>
</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy jeBHqu gcushC"><div><h3 class="sc-kEqXSa iXmHCl"> <!-- -->Request samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-cxNHIi gxohHo" </span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy jeBHqu gcushC"></div></div></div><div id="tag/data" data-section-id="tag/data" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs jBVWZw"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/data" aria-label="tag/data"></a>data</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN fydXJm"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt redoc-markdown "><p>Work with table data, using a (now deprecated) columnar format. We now recommend the <code>records</code> endpoints.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/data/operation/getTableData" data-section-id="tag/data/operation/getTableData" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/getTableData" id="operation/getTableData" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM ejDbYC"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/data/operation/getTableData" aria-label="tag/data/operation/getTableData"></a>Fetch data from a table<!-- --> <span type="warning" class="sc-bqGGPW eSYQnm"> Deprecated </span></h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN cjZEpp http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT gWMowg">/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/data</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dFHjgH"><span>https://{gristhost}/api</span>/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/data</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGkqmO hCTIhr"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"><p>Deprecated in favor of <code>records</code> endpoints. We have no immediate plans to remove these endpoints, but consider <code>records</code> a better starting point for new projects.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf dVTqCh"><span class="sc-dsXzNU A-DJqO"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>normalized table name (see <code>TABLE ID</code> in Raw Data) or numeric row ID in <code>_grist_Tables</code></p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="X-Limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">X-Limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Same as <code>limit</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh lbYftx"><svg class="sc-dIsUp dqYXmg" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC kdwQRp"><p>Cells from the table</p>

</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy jeBHqu gcushC"><div><h3 class="sc-kEqXSa iXmHCl"> <!-- -->Request samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-cxNHIi gxohHo" data-rttabs="true"><ul class="react-tabs__tab-list" role="tablist"><li class="react-tabs__tab react-tabs__tab--selected" role="tab" id="react-tabs-92" aria-selected="true" aria-disabled="false" aria-controls="react-tabs-93" tabindex="0" data-rttab="true">Payload</li></ul><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel react-tabs__tab-panel--selected" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-93" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-92"><div><div class="sc-Arkif jojbRz"><span class="sc-cOifOu gWaFEV">Content type</span><div class="sc-bBjRSN cNprXd">application/json</div></div><div class="sc-jgPyTC dSaTNC"><div class="sc-jNnpgg esZIbL"><div class="sc-giAqHp bBhLhz"><button><div class="sc-carFqZ UksDl">Copy</div></button></div><div class="sc-iJCRrE jCdxGr sc-dPaNzc ldDruB"><div class="redoc-json"><code><button class="collapser" aria-label="collapse"></button><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><ul class="array collapsible"><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="token number">101</span>,</div></li><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="token number">102</span>,</div></li><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="token number">103</span></div></li></ul><span class="token punctuation">]</span></code></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/attachments" data-section-id="tag/attachments" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs jBVWZw"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/attachments" aria-label="tag/attachments"></a>attachments</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN fydXJm"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt redoc-markdown "><p>Documents may include attached files. Data records can refer to these using a column of type <code>Attachments</code>.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments" data-section-id="tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/listAttachments" id="operation/listAttachments" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM ejDbYC"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments" aria-label="tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments"></a>List metadata of all attachments in a doc<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="get" class="sc-fmdNqN cjZEpp http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT gWMowg">/docs/{docId}/attachments</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dFHjgH"><span>https://{gristhost}/api</span>/docs/{docId}/attachments</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf dVTqCh"><span class="sc-dsXzNU A-DJqO"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="X-Limit"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">X-Limit</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-laZMeE jWaWWE"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-laZMeE sc-ckTSus jWaWWE dcaRiz">5</span></div><div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Same as <code>limit</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh lbYftx"><svg class="sc-dIsUp dqYXmg" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC kdwQRp"><p>List of attachment metadata records. class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM ejDbYC"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/attachments/operation/removeUnusedAttachments" aria-label="tag/attachments/operation/removeUnusedAttachments"></a>Delete unused attachments from the document<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="post" class="sc-fmdNqN jNYsSj http-verb post">post</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT gWMowg">/docs/{docId}/attachments/removeUnused</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dFHjgH"><span>https://{gristhost}/api</span>/docs/{docId}/attachments/removeUnused</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGkqmO hCTIhr"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"><p>When an uploaded attachment is no longer used in a Grist document,  it&#39;s retained for a period of time in case it&#39;s needed again (e.g. to facilitate an &quot;undo&quot;).
This removes all of these retained attachments, reducing the amount of storage used. This is particularly useful if a document has hit its attachment storage limit.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf dVTqCh"><span class="sc-dsXzNU A-DJqO"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="expiredOnly"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">expiredOnly</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Only remove attachments that haven&#39;t been used for a period of time. This duration is set by host of the Grist instance.</p>

</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-jSFjdj sc-gKAaRy jeBHqu gcushC"></div></div></div><div id="tag/webhooks" data-section-id="tag/webhooks" class="sc-eCApnc lpoiLM"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs jBVWZw"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/webhooks" aria-label="tag/webhooks"></a>webhooks</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN fydXJm"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt redoc-markdown "><p>Document changes can trigger requests to URLs called webhooks.</p>

Must be a single SELECT statement, with no trailing semicolon. WITH clauses are permitted. All Grist documents are currently SQLite databases, and the SQL query is interpreted and run by SQLite, with various defensive measures. Statements that would modify the database are not supported.</p>

</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="timeout"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">timeout</span></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">number</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>Timeout after which operations on the document will be interrupted. The default cannot be exceeded, only reduced.</p>

fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h1 class="sc-fujyAs jBVWZw"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/users" aria-label="tag/users"></a>users</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hKFxyN fydXJm"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt redoc-markdown "><p>Grist users.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/users/paths/~1users~1{userId}/delete" data-section-id="tag/users/paths/~1users~1{userId}/delete" class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM ejDbYC"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/users/paths/~1users~1{userId}/delete" aria-label="tag/users/paths/~1users~1{userId}/delete"></a>Delete a user from Grist<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="delete" class="sc-fmdNqN kDKLNl http-verb delete">delete</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT gWMowg">/users/{userId}</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dFHjgH"><span>https://{gristhost}/api</span>/users/{userId}</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGkqmO hCTIhr"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"><p>This action also deletes the user&#39;s personal organisation and all the workspaces and documents it contains.
Currently, only the users themselves are allowed to delete their own accounts.</p>
<p> <strong>This action cannot be undone, please be cautious when using this endpoint</strong> </p>
</div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf dVTqCh"><span class="sc-dsXzNU A-DJqO"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="userId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">userId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">integer</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>A user id</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-cBoqAE eKyrDP">application/json</span></h5><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"></div><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="name"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">name</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>The user&#39;s name to delete (for confirmation, to avoid deleting the wrong account).</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh jUGDyD" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC kdwQRp"><p>The account has been deleted successfully</p>
</span></button></div><div><button class="sc-htmcrh cGFwjB" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">400<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC kdwQRp"><p>The passed user name does not match the one retrieved from the database given the passed user id</p>
</span></button></div><div><button class="sc-htmcrh cGFwjB" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">403<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC kdwQRp"><p>The caller is not allowed to delete this account</p>

class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/updateUserById" id="operation/updateUserById" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM ejDbYC"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/scim/operation/updateUserById" aria-label="tag/scim/operation/updateUserById"></a>Update a user by ID<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="put" class="sc-fmdNqN gpyjOQ http-verb put">put</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT gWMowg">/scim/v2/Users/{userId}</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dFHjgH"><span>https://{gristhost}/api</span>/scim/v2/Users/{userId}</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGkqmO hCTIhr"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"><p>  This operation override all the user&#39;s information. In order to pass only some properties to update, please use <a href="#tag/scim/operation/patchUserById">PATCH</a> instead.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf dVTqCh"><span class="sc-dsXzNU A-DJqO"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT fQMiLF doEmFO" kind="field" title="userId"><span class="sc-iemWCZ bxBsrD"></span><span class="property-name">userId</span><div class="sc-oeezt sc-hhIiOg dLCGMn hIkHYw">required</div></td><td class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">integer</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"><p>A user id</p>

class="sc-eCApnc khndJD"><div data-section-id="operation/patchUserById" id="operation/patchUserById" class="sc-iCoGMd fStpoi"><div class="sc-hKFxyN fvvWDw"><h2 class="sc-pNWdM ejDbYC"><a class="sc-crzoAE iUxAWq" href="#tag/scim/operation/patchUserById" aria-label="tag/scim/operation/patchUserById"></a>Partially update a user by ID<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-EZqKI fWsqvQ"><button class="sc-eEVmNe hyDbyC"><span type="patch" class="sc-fmdNqN hphDwZ http-verb patch">patch</span><span class="sc-jXcxbT gWMowg">/scim/v2/Users/{userId}</span><svg class="sc-dIsUp izTTdU" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-ljsmAU flIrdF"><div class="sc-jlZJtj fQkroN"><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr dmgxOH"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-dTSzeu dFHjgH"><span>https://{gristhost}/api</span>/scim/v2/Users/{userId}</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-fcmMJX cvfxAX"><div class="sc-jUfyBS bhDyou"><h5 class="sc-iqAclL sc-fuISkM eONCmm hZIgic">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-dIsUp iPqByX" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-jQAxuV ccffaZ"><span class="sc-daBunf dVTqCh"><span class="sc-dsXzNU A-DJqO"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hHEiqL VCQHZ"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-hBMUJo sc-fFSPTT class="sc-bkbkJK gawiqV"><div><div><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-iNiQyp jWaWWE jrLlAa"></span><span class="sc-laZMeE sc-jffHpj jWaWWE cThoNa">integer</span></div> <div><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP </div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h5 class="sc-iqAclL eONCmm">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-cBoqAE eKyrDP">application/scim+json</span></h5><div class="sc-iJCRrE sc-ciSkZP jCdxGr eIaKBt"><p>Data for the partial update of the user.</p>

</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fIxmyt DvFer">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-htmcrh lbYftx"><svg class="sc-dIsUp dqYXmg" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC kdwQRp"><p>Users retrieved based on search criteria.</p>
</span></button></div><div><button class="sc-htmcrh cGFwjB" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">400<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC kdwQRp"><p>Bad request.</p>
</span></button></div><div><button class="sc-htmcrh cGFwjB" disabled=""><strong class="sc-fWWYYk cMoEZ">401<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-jcwpoC kdwQRp"><p>Unauthenticated</p>

For example: '-1.23', '12678967.543233', '+100000.00', '210'.\n\nThe following special string values are permitted (case does not need to be respected):\n  - NaN: not a number\n  - INF: positive infinity\n  - -INF: negative infinity\n\nA number `MAY` also have a trailing:\n  - exponent: this `MUST` consist of an E followed by an optional + or - sign followed by one or more decimal digits (0-9)\n  - percentage: the percentage sign: `%`.
